[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A fuzzer-triggered stack overflow occurred during regular-expression matching in    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the Java regex engine while extracting extended properties from an XLSX file. The   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         overflow manifested as deep, repetitive recursion in various                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `java.util.regex.Pattern` matching methods, ultimately causing the JVM to exhaust   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         its call stack. The issue was detected in the context of Apache POI’s               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor` handling of the `AppVersion` property.               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           A `StackOverflowError` was raised in the regex engine [1m([0m`java.util.regex.Pattern`[1m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         as it processed a pattern repeatedly in deeply nested matching routines. The        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         exception surfaced during XML parsing of a spreadsheet’s extended properties,       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         specifically within the `handleAppVersion` method of the                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.ExtendedPropertiesHandler`.                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability Type                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           FuzzerSecurityIssue: Stack overflow.                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Important Observations                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The stack trace shows thousands of recursive calls through                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Pattern$Ques.match`, `Pattern$Loop.match`, `Pattern$GroupHead.match`,              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Pattern$GroupTail.match`, and related methods, indicating catastrophic             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         backtracking or unbounded recursion in the regex engine.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The overflow occurs during SAX-based XML parsing [1m([0mXerces[1m)[0m when the extractor    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         processes application version strings from the document.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The fuzzer harness entry point [1m([0m`POIXSSFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[1m)[0m drives the  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         vulnerable code path but is not the root cause.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Code Areas for Investigation                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m.                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `org.apache.poi.xssf.extractor.XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.ExtendedPropertiesHandl [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         er.handleAppVersion` [1m([0maround line [1;36m530[0m[1m)[0m – where the regex is applied to the version  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         string.                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. Any regex pattern definitions used by the extractor for matching version or    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         other extended property values.                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. SAX parsing integration in `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps` and [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         related methods to understand how input data reaches the regex engine.              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. The `java.util.regex.Pattern` implementation [1m([0mthough part of the JDK[1m)[0m to map   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the observed recursion to specific pattern constructs in use.                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         > No root-cause analysis or remediation steps are provided; this report focuses     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         solely on documenting and outlining the issue.                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Here is the initial issue log of the codebase:                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m<[0m[1;95missue[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFuzzerSecurityIssue: Stack overflow[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m java.util.regex.Pattern$Ques.match [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPattern.jav[0m[1;92ma:4[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m229[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m449[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mprops.getProperties[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.isSetAppVersion[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `MAJOR_VERSION_PATTERN` regex [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m([0m[39m-?[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\d[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m*[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\[0m[1;35m.[0m[1;39m([0m[39m\\dc?[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor uses nested, unbounded quantifiers. This leads to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcatastrophic backtracking and unbounded recursion inside the JDK’s regex engine [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen fed maliciously long or repetitive version strings, ultimately triggering a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`StackOverflowError`.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerable code path is exclusively in the SAX-based handler’s [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`handleAppVersion` method:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Matcher m = [0m[1;35mMAJOR_VERSION_PATTERN.matcher[0m[1;39m([0m[39mappVersionString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mm.find[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mtext.append[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"MajorVersion: "[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.append[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mm.group[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.append[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"\n"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The non-SAX extractor [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mPOIXMLProperties.getAppVersion[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m does not use regex;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit simply returns the raw string, and any downstream splitting or parsing is [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandled without recursion.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Critical Logic[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only functional requirement here is to extract and emit the “major [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mversion” component [0m[1;39m([0m[39meverything before the first `.`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m of the `appVersionString`.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other behaviors—ignoring empty strings, resetting the buffer, appending to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe output—must remain unchanged.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Patch Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Remove [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor deprecate[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m the static `MAJOR_VERSION_PATTERN` field, since it is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno longer needed.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.ExtendedPropertiesHandler.handleAppVersion[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace the regex-based matching with a simple, linear-time string [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private void [0m[1;35mhandleAppVersion[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            String appVersionString = [0m[1;35mappVersionBuffer.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mappVersionString.isEmpty[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                return;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Split on the first dot [0m[1;39m([0m[39m.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, limit to [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m parts to capture major [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mversion only[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            String[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m parts = [0m[1;35mappVersionString.split[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"\\."[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            String majorVersion = parts[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m will be entire string if no dot [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpresent[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mtext.append[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"MajorVersion: "[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35m.append[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmajorVersion[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35m.append[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"\n"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mappVersionBuffer.setLength[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Remove any imports related to `java.util.regex.Pattern` in this class if no [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlonger used.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification & Impact[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Linear-time `String.split` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith a limit argument[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`String.indexOf`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`substring` has no backtracking, eliminating the vulnerability.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Behavior is identical for valid version strings:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `[0m[32m"1.2.3"[0m[39m` → `parts[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[32m"1"[0m[39m`  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `[0m[32m"-10.5"[0m[39m` → `parts[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[32m"-10"[0m[39m`  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `[0m[32m"42"[0m[39m`   → `parts[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[32m"42"[0m[39m`  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For empty input, logic still returns early.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side Effects: [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m on non-malicious inputs. Existing unit tests or integration[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests that verify output for `MajorVersion:` will continue to pass.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to fuzzing harnesses, SAX parsers, or any external [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibraries.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Validation[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add unit tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif not already present[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to verify edge cases:  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • No dot: entire string is major version  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Leading/trailing dots: empty major version or correct prefix  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Negative numbers  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Very long numeric strings [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto ensure linear-time behavior[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing test suite to ensure no regressions.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar logic exists in the non-SAX extractor:  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     String[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m parts = [0m[1;35mappVersionString.split[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"\\."[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach is already proven safe and efficient within the Apache POI [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
